   120 +    "# ── Main user-level query (aggregated from Authors + CleanedModData + GameCategories) ──\n",
   121 +    "query = \"\"\"\n",
   122 +    "SELECT \n",
   123 +    "    a.member_id,\n",
   124 +    "    a.joined, \n",
   125 +    "    a.last_active,\n",
   126 +    "    MIN(c.created_timestamp)  AS first_mod_created_date,\n",
   127 +    "    MAX(c.created_timestamp)  AS last_mod_created_date,\n",
   128 +    "    DATEDIFF(DAY, a.joined, a.last_active) AS active_days,\n",
   129 +    "    a.recognized_author,\n",
   130 +    "    a.mod_count                             AS published_mod_count,\n",
   131 +    "    a.owned_mod_count - a.mod_count         AS unpublished_mod_count,\n",
   132 +    "    a.collection_count,\n",
   133 +    "    a.contributed_mod_count,\n",
   134 +    "    a.owned_mod_count                       AS all_mods_count,\n",
   135 +    "    a.endorsements_given,\n",
   136 +    "    a.posts,\n",
   137 +    "    a.kudos,\n",
   138 +    "    a.views,\n",
   139 +    "    a.donations_enabled,\n",
   140 +    "    COUNT(DISTINCT c.domain_name)           AS total_domains,\n",
   141 +    "    COUNT(DISTINCT e.new_group_category)    AS total_categories,\n",
   142 +    "    SUM(ISNULL(c.endorsement_count, 0))     AS endorsements_received,\n",
   143 +    "    SUM(CASE WHEN c.contains_adult_content = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS adult_content_count,\n",
   144 +    "    SUM(ISNULL(c.mod_downloads, 0))         AS all_mod_downloads,\n",
   145 +    "    SUM(ISNULL(c.mod_unique_downloads, 0))  AS all_unique_mod_downloads\n",
   146 +    "FROM dbo.Authors AS a \n",
   147 +    "LEFT JOIN dbo.CleanedModData  AS c ON c.member_id = a.member_id\n",
   148 +    "LEFT JOIN dbo.GameCategories  AS e ON e.category_id = c.category_id AND e.game_id = c.game_id\n",
   149 +    "WHERE a.deleted = 0 \n",
   150 +    "    AND a.last_active IS NOT NULL \n",
   151 +    "    AND a.last_active >= '2024-01-01'\n",
   152 +    "GROUP BY \n",
   153 +    "    a.member_id, a.joined, a.last_active, a.recognized_author,\n",
   154 +    "    a.mod_count, a.owned_mod_count, a.collection_count,\n",
   155 +    "    a.contributed_mod_count, a.endorsements_given, a.posts,\n",
   156 +    "    a.kudos, a.views, a.donations_enabled\n",
   157 +    "\"\"\"\n",
   158 +    "\n",
   159 +    "print('Loading data from SQL...')\n",
   160 +    "df_raw = pd.read_sql(query, engine)\n",
   161 +    "N_RAW = 1_028_417  # Total user records before filtering (from paper)\n",
   162 +    "print(f'Rows returned (active, non-deleted, last_active >= 2024-01-01): {len(df_raw):,}')"
   163 +   ]
   164 +  },
   165 +  {
   166 +   "cell_type": "code",
   167 +   "execution_count": null,
   168 +   "metadata": {},
   169 +   "outputs": [],
   170 +   "source": [
   171 +    "# ── Apply inclusion criterion 3: at least 1 mod ──\n",
   172 +    "df = df_raw[df_raw['all_mods_count'] > 0].copy()\n",
   173 +    "\n",
   174 +    "# Date conversions\n",
   175 +    "df['first_mod_created_date'] = pd.to_datetime(df['first_mod_created_date'], unit='s')\n",
   176 +    "df['last_mod_created_date']  = pd.to_datetime(df['last_mod_created_date'],  unit='s', errors='coerce')\n",
   177 +    "df['joined']      = pd.to_datetime(df['joined'])\n",
   178 +    "df['last_active']  = pd.to_datetime(df['last_active'])\n",
   179 +    "\n",
   180 +    "# Derived temporal features\n",
   181 +    "df['mod_creation_days_since_joined'] = (df['first_mod_created_date'] - df['joined']).dt.days\n",
   182 +    "df['activity_span_days'] = (df['last_mod_created_date'] - df['first_mod_created_date']).dt.days\n",
   183 +    "df['activity_span_days'] = df['activity_span_days'].clip(lower=0)\n",
   184 +    "\n",
   185 +    "N_FINAL = len(df)\n",
   186 +    "print(f'Final analytic sample: N = {N_FINAL:,}')"
   187 +   ]
   188 +  },
   189 +  {
   190 +   "cell_type": "markdown",
   191 +   "metadata": {},
   192 +   "source": [
   193 +    "### 2.1 Sample Description  \n",
   194 +    "**Paper §3.2** — Three sequential inclusion criteria"
   195 +   ]
   196 +  },
   197 +  {
   198 +   "cell_type": "code",
   199 +   "execution_count": null,
   200 +   "metadata": {},
   201 +   "outputs": [],
   202 +   "source": [
   203 +    "# ── Table: Sample filtering pipeline ──\n",
   204 +    "sample_pipeline = pd.DataFrame({\n",
   205 +    "    'Stage': [\n",
   206 +    "        '1. Raw user-level records (Authors × CleanedModData)',\n",
   207 +    "        '2. Non-deleted, last_active ≥ 2024-01-01',\n",
   208 +    "        '3. At least one mod (creators only)'\n",
   209 +    "    ],\n",
   210 +    "    'N': [\n",
   211 +    "        f'{N_RAW:,}',\n",
   212 +    "        f'{len(df_raw):,}',\n",
   213 +    "        f'{N_FINAL:,}'\n",
   214 +    "    ],\n",
   215 +    "    'Dropped': [\n",
   216 +    "        '—',\n",
   217 +    "        f'{N_RAW - len(df_raw):,}',\n",
   218 +    "        f'{len(df_raw) - N_FINAL:,}'\n",
   219 +    "    ]\n",
   220 +    "})\n",
   221 +    "show(sample_pipeline, 'Sample Filtering Pipeline (Paper §3.2)')"
   222 +   ]
   223 +  },
   224 +  {

   227 +   "metadata": {},
   228 +   "outputs": [],
   229 +   "source": [
   230 +    "# ── Table: Descriptive statistics for the 13 raw features ──\n",
   231 +    "raw_features = [\n",
   232 +    "    'published_mod_count', 'unpublished_mod_count', 'all_mods_count',\n",
   233 +    "    'endorsements_given', 'posts', 'kudos', 'views',\n",
   234 +    "    'endorsements_received', 'adult_content_count',\n",

   237 +    "]\n",
   238 +    "\n",
   239 +    "raw_desc = df[raw_features].describe().T\n",
   240 +    "raw_desc['skewness'] = df[raw_features].skew()\n",
   241 +    "raw_desc = raw_desc[['count', 'mean', 'std', 'min', '25%', '50%', '75%', 'max', 'skewness']]\n",
   242 +    "raw_desc = raw_desc.round(2)\n",
   243 +    "show(raw_desc, 'Descriptive Statistics — Raw Features (before transformation)')"
   244 +   ]
   245 +  },
   246 +  {
   247 +   "cell_type": "markdown",
   248 +   "metadata": {},
   249 +   "source": [
   250 +    "---\n",
   251 +    "## 3. Preprocessing & Skewness Reduction  \n",
   252 +    "**Paper §3.3 / Appendix D2 (Table: Skewness) / Appendix D9 (Table: Preprocessing)**"
   253 +   ]
   254 +  },
   255 +  {
   256 +   "cell_type": "code",
   257 +   "execution_count": null,
   258 +   "metadata": {},
   259 +   "outputs": [],
   260 +   "source": [
   261 +    "def apply_transformations(df):\n",
   262 +    "    \"\"\"\n",
   263 +    "    Apply feature-specific transformations to reduce skewness.\n",
   264 +    "    \n",
   265 +    "    - Log(1+x): endorsements_given, posts, kudos\n",
   266 +    "    - Winsorise [2%, 98%] + cube-root: views\n",
   267 +    "    - Yeo-Johnson: published_mod_count, unpublished_mod_count, all_mods_count,\n",
   268 +    "                   endorsements_received, adult_content_count,\n",
   269 +    "                   all_mod_downloads, all_unique_mod_downloads\n",
   270 +    "    - None: mod_creation_days_since_joined, last_mod_created_date\n",
   271 +    "    \"\"\"\n",
   272 +    "    out = df.copy()\n",
   273 +    "    \n",
   274 +    "    # Log transform\n",
   275 +    "    for col in ['endorsements_given', 'posts', 'kudos']:\n",
   276 +    "        out[col] = np.log1p(df[col].clip(lower=0))\n",
   277 +    "    \n",
   278 +    "    # Winsorise + cube-root\n",
   279 +    "    out['views'] = winsorize(df['views'], limits=[0.02, 0.02])\n",
   280 +    "    out['views'] = np.cbrt(out['views'])\n",
   281 +    "    \n",
   282 +    "    # Yeo-Johnson\n",
   283 +    "    yj_cols = [\n",
   284 +    "        'published_mod_count', 'unpublished_mod_count', 'all_mods_count',\n",
   285 +    "        'endorsements_received', 'adult_content_count',\n",
   286 +    "        'all_mod_downloads', 'all_unique_mod_downloads'\n",
   287 +    "    ]\n",
   288 +    "    for col in yj_cols:\n",
   289 +    "        out[col], _ = yeojohnson(df[col] + 1)\n",
   290 +    "    \n",
   291 +    "    return out\n",
   292 +    "\n",
   293 +    "df_transformed = apply_transformations(df)\n",
   294 +    "print('Transformations applied.')"
   295 +   ]
   296 +  },
   297 +  {
   298 +   "cell_type": "code",
   299 +   "execution_count": null,
   300 +   "metadata": {},
   301 +   "outputs": [],
   302 +   "source": [
   303 +    "# ── Table: Skewness before & after transformation (Appendix D2 / D9) ──\n",
   304 +    "transform_map = {\n",
   305 +    "    'published_mod_count':    'Yeo-Johnson',\n",
   306 +    "    'unpublished_mod_count':  'Yeo-Johnson',\n",
   307 +    "    'all_mods_count':         'Yeo-Johnson',\n",
   308 +    "    'endorsements_given':     'log(1+x)',\n",
   309 +    "    'posts':                  'log(1+x)',\n",
   310 +    "    'kudos':                  'log(1+x)',\n",
   311 +    "    'views':                  'Winsorise + cube-root',\n",
   312 +    "    'endorsements_received':  'Yeo-Johnson',\n",
   313 +    "    'adult_content_count':    'Yeo-Johnson',\n",
   314 +    "    'all_mod_downloads':      'Yeo-Johnson',\n",
   315 +    "    'all_unique_mod_downloads': 'Yeo-Johnson',\n",
   316 +    "    'mod_creation_days_since_joined': 'None',\n",
   317 +    "}\n",
   318 +    "\n",
   319 +    "skew_table = pd.DataFrame({\n",
   320 +    "    'Feature': list(transform_map.keys()),\n",
   321 +    "    'Original Skewness': [df[c].skew() for c in transform_map],\n",
   322 +    "    'Transformation': list(transform_map.values()),\n",
   323 +    "    'Post-Transform Skewness': [df_transformed[c].skew() for c in transform_map]\n",
   324 +    "})\n",
   325 +    "skew_table['Original Skewness'] = skew_table['Original Skewness'].round(4)\n",
   326 +    "skew_table['Post-Transform Skewness'] = skew_table['Post-Transform Skewness'].round(4)\n",
   327 +    "\n",
   328 +    "show(skew_table, 'Skewness Before & After Transformation (Paper Table D2/D9)')"
   329 +   ]
   330 +  },
   331 +  {
   332 +   "cell_type": "markdown",
   333 +   "metadata": {},
   334 +   "source": [
   335 +    "---\n",
   336 +    "## 4. Feature Selection, Scaling & PCA  \n",
   337 +    "**Paper §3.4 / Appendix A1 (Scree Plot), A2 (Loadings Heatmap & Table)**"
   338 +   ]
   339 +  },
   340 +  {

   343 +   "metadata": {},

   349 +    "    'unpublished_mod_count',\n",
   350 +    "    'all_mods_count',\n",
   351 +    "    'endorsements_given',\n",
   352 +    "    'posts',\n",
   353 +    "    'kudos',\n",
   354 +    "    'views',\n",
   355 +    "    'endorsements_received',\n",
   356 +    "    'adult_content_count',\n",
   357 +    "    'all_mod_downloads',\n",
   358 +    "    'all_unique_mod_downloads',\n",
   359 +    "    'mod_creation_days_since_joined',\n",

   361 +    "]\n",
   362 +    "\n",
   363 +    "# Convert last_mod_created_date to numeric (days since earliest)\n",

   365 +    "    pd.to_datetime(df['last_mod_created_date']) - pd.to_datetime(df['last_mod_created_date']).min()\n",
   366 +    ") / pd.Timedelta(days=1)\n",

   387 +    "cumvar = np.cumsum(pca_full.explained_variance_ratio_)\n",
   388 +    "\n",
   389 +    "# Scree plot (Appendix A1)\n",
   390 +    "fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(10, 6))\n",
   391 +    "ax.plot(range(1, len(cumvar)+1), cumvar, 'bo-')\n",
   392 +    "ax.axhline(y=0.95, color='r', ls='--', label='95% variance')\n",
   393 +    "ax.set_xlabel('Number of Components')\n",
   394 +    "ax.set_ylabel('Cumulative Explained Variance')\n",
   395 +    "ax.set_title('PCA Scree Plot (Appendix A1)')\n",
   396 +    "ax.legend()\n",
   397 +    "ax.grid(True)\n",

   400 +    "plt.show()\n",
   401 +    "\n",
   402 +    "n_components_95 = np.argmax(cumvar >= 0.95) + 1\n",
   403 +    "print(f'Components for ≥95% variance: {n_components_95}')"
   404 +   ]

   463 +    "---\n",
   464 +    "## 5. Devotion Score  \n",
   465 +    "**Paper §4.1 / Table 1 (Descriptive stats) / Appendix B1 (Histogram), B2 (Summary stats)**\n",
   466 +    "\n",
   467 +    "Formula:  \n",
   468 +    "$w_j = \\sum_{k=1}^{K} \\lambda_k |L_{kj}|$ &emsp; then &emsp; $D_i = \\sum_{j=1}^{p} w_j \\tilde{x}_{ij}$
       +"
   469 +   ]
   470 +  },
   471 +  {
   472 +   "cell_type": "code",
   473 +   "execution_count": null,
   474 +   "metadata": {},
   475 +   "outputs": [],
   476 +   "source": [
   477 +    "# ── Compute variance-weighted feature importance ──\n",
   478 +    "loadings_abs = np.abs(pca.components_)          # (7, 13)\n",
   479 +    "feature_weights = np.dot(explained_variance, loadings_abs)  # (13,)\n",
   480 +    "\n",
   481 +    "# ── Table: Feature weights ──\n",
   482 +    "weight_table = pd.DataFrame({\n",
   483 +    "    'Feature': analysis_features,\n",
   484 +    "    'PCA-Derived Weight': feature_weights\n",
   485 +    "}).sort_values('PCA-Derived Weight', ascending=False).reset_index(drop=True)\n",
   486 +    "weight_table['PCA-Derived Weight'] = weight_table['PCA-Derived Weight'].round(4)\n",
   487 +    "\n",
   488 +    "show(weight_table, 'Feature Importance Weights (Equation 1)')"
   489 +   ]
   490 +  },
   491 +  {
   492 +   "cell_type": "code",
   493 +   "execution_count": null,
   494 +   "metadata": {},
   495 +   "outputs": [],
   496 +   "source": [
   497 +    "# ── Compute Devotion Score for each user ──\n",
   498 +    "devotion_scores = np.dot(data_scaled, feature_weights)\n",
   499 +    "\n",
   500 +    "# Attach to analysis df and to original df\n",
   501 +    "df_analysis_idx = df_analysis.index\n",
   502 +    "df.loc[df_analysis_idx, 'Devotion_Score'] = devotion_scores"
   503 +   ]
   504 +  },
   505 +  {
   506 +   "cell_type": "code",
   507 +   "execution_count": null,
   508 +   "metadata": {},
   509 +   "outputs": [],
   510 +   "source": [
   511 +    "# ── Table: Devotion Score summary statistics (Paper Table 1 / Appendix B2) ──\n",
   512 +    "ds = pd.Series(devotion_scores)\n",
   513 +    "\n",
   514 +    "devotion_summary = pd.DataFrame({\n",
   515 +    "    'Statistic': [\n",
   516 +    "        'Count', 'Mean', 'Std. Deviation', 'Min',\n",
   517 +    "        '25th Percentile (Q1)', 'Median (Q2)', '75th Percentile (Q3)',\n",
   518 +    "        'Max', 'Skewness', '95th Percentile'\n",
   519 +    "    ],\n",
   520 +    "    'Value': [\n",
   521 +    "        f'{len(ds):,}',\n",
   522 +    "        f'{ds.mean():.3f}',\n",
   523 +    "        f'{ds.std():.3f}',\n",
   524 +    "        f'{ds.min():.3f}',\n",
   525 +    "        f'{ds.quantile(0.25):.3f}',\n",
   526 +    "        f'{ds.median():.3f}',\n",
   527 +    "        f'{ds.quantile(0.75):.3f}',\n",
   528 +    "        f'{ds.max():.3f}',\n",
   529 +    "        f'{ds.skew():.3f}',\n",
   530 +    "        f'{ds.quantile(0.95):.3f}'\n",
   531 +    "    ]\n",
   532 +    "})\n",
   533 +    "\n",
   534 +    "show(devotion_summary, 'Devotion Score — Summary Statistics (Paper Table 1 / Appendix B2)')"
   535 +   ]
   536 +  },
   537 +  {
   538 +   "cell_type": "code",
   539 +   "execution_count": null,
   540 +   "metadata": {},
   541 +   "outputs": [],
   542 +   "source": [
   543 +    "# ── Figure: Devotion Score histogram (Appendix B1) ──\n",
   544 +    "fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(10, 6))\n",
   545 +    "ax.hist(devotion_scores, bins=50, edgecolor='black', alpha=0.7)\n",
   546 +    "ax.axvline(ds.mean(), color='r', ls='--', label=f'Mean = {ds.mean():.2f}')\n",
   547 +    "ax.axvline(ds.median(), color='g', ls='--', label=f'Median = {ds.median():.2f}')\n",
   548 +    "ax.set_xlabel('Devotion Score')\n",

   553 +    "fig.savefig('distribution_devotion.png', dpi=300, bbox_inches='tight')\n",
   554 +    "plt.show()"
   555 +   ]
   556 +  },
   557 +  {
   558 +   "cell_type": "markdown",
   559 +   "metadata": {},
   560 +   "source": [
   561 +    "---\n",
   562 +    "## 6. K-Means Clustering  \n",
   563 +    "**Paper §4.2 / Appendix C1 (Cluster plot) / Appendix D1 (Silhouette)**"
   564 +   ]
   565 +  },
   566 +  {
   567 +   "cell_type": "code",
   568 +   "execution_count": null,
   569 +   "metadata": {},
   570 +   "outputs": [],
   571 +   "source": [
   572 +    "# ── Elbow + silhouette analysis ──\n",
   573 +    "k_range = range(2, 10)\n",
   574 +    "inertias = []\n",
   575 +    "sil_scores = []\n",
   576 +    "\n",
   577 +    "for k in k_range:\n",
   578 +    "    km = KMeans(n_clusters=k, random_state=42, n_init=10)\n",
   579 +    "    labels = km.fit_predict(pca_data)\n",
   580 +    "    inertias.append(km.inertia_)\n",
   581 +    "    sil_scores.append(silhouette_score(pca_data, labels))\n",
   582 +    "\n",
   583 +    "fig, axes = plt.subplots(1, 2, figsize=(14, 5))\n",
   584 +    "axes[0].plot(k_range, inertias, 'bo-')\n",
   585 +    "axes[0].set_xlabel('k'); axes[0].set_ylabel('Inertia'); axes[0].set_title('Elbow Method')\n",
   586 +    "axes[1].plot(k_range, sil_scores, 'go-')\n",
   587 +    "axes[1].set_xlabel('k'); axes[1].set_ylabel('Silhouette Score'); axes[1].set_title('Silhouette Analysis')\
       +n",
   588 +    "fig.tight_layout()\n",
   589 +    "plt.show()\n",
   590 +    "\n",
   591 +    "# ── Table: Silhouette scores by k ──\n",
   592 +    "sil_table = pd.DataFrame({'k': list(k_range), 'Silhouette Score': [round(s, 3) for s in sil_scores]})\n",
   593 +    "show(sil_table, 'Silhouette Scores by k')"
   594 +   ]
   595 +  },
   596 +  {
   597 +   "cell_type": "code",
   598 +   "execution_count": null,

   606 +    "\n",
   607 +    "sil_final = silhouette_score(pca_data, raw_labels)\n",

   609 +   ]

   925 +    "---\n",
   926 +    "## 12. Silhouette Comparison Across Methods  \n",
   927 +    "**Appendix D1**"
   928 +   ]
   929 +  },
   930 +  {
   931 +   "cell_type": "code",
   932 +   "execution_count": null,
   933 +   "metadata": {},
   934 +   "outputs": [],
   935 +   "source": [
   936 +    "# ── Compare clustering methods (Appendix D1) ──\n",
   937 +    "results = []\n",
   938 +    "\n",
   939 +    "# K-Means on 7 PCs (already computed)\n",
   940 +    "results.append(('K-Means (7 PC)', sil_final, 'Final clustering input'))\n",
   941 +    "\n",
   942 +    "# K-Means on 2 PCs (for interpretability)\n",
   943 +    "pca2 = PCA(n_components=2).fit_transform(data_scaled)\n",
   944 +    "km2 = KMeans(n_clusters=4, random_state=42, n_init=10).fit_predict(pca2)\n",
   945 +    "results.append(('K-Means (2 PC)', round(silhouette_score(pca2, km2), 2), 'For interpretability only'))\n",
   946 +    "\n",
   947 +    "# DBSCAN\n",
   948 +    "db_labels = DBSCAN(eps=1.0, min_samples=10).fit_predict(pca_data)\n",
   949 +    "if len(set(db_labels) - {-1}) >= 2:\n",
   950 +    "    mask = db_labels != -1\n",
   951 +    "    db_sil = round(silhouette_score(pca_data[mask], db_labels[mask]), 2)\n",
   952 +    "else:\n",
   953 +    "    db_sil = 'N/A (< 2 clusters)'\n",
   954 +    "results.append(('DBSCAN', db_sil, 'eps=1.0, min_samples=10'))\n",
   955 +    "\n",
   956 +    "# GMM\n",
   957 +    "gmm_labels = GaussianMixture(n_components=4, random_state=42).fit_predict(pca_data)\n",
   958 +    "gmm_sil = round(silhouette_score(pca_data, gmm_labels), 2)\n",
   959 +    "results.append(('GMM', gmm_sil, 'Moderate separation'))\n",
   960 +    "\n",
   961 +    "# Try HDBSCAN if available\n",
   962 +    "try:\n",
   963 +    "    from hdbscan import HDBSCAN as HDBSCANCluster\n",
   964 +    "    hdb = HDBSCANCluster(min_cluster_size=50).fit(pca_data)\n",
   965 +    "    hdb_labels = hdb.labels_\n",
   966 +    "    if len(set(hdb_labels) - {-1}) >= 2:\n",
   967 +    "        mask_h = hdb_labels != -1\n",
   968 +    "        hdb_sil = round(silhouette_score(pca_data[mask_h], hdb_labels[mask_h]), 2)\n",
   969 +    "    else:\n",
   970 +    "        hdb_sil = 'N/A'\n",
   971 +    "    results.append(('HDBSCAN', hdb_sil, 'min_cluster_size=50'))\n",
   972 +    "except ImportError:\n",
   973 +    "    results.append(('HDBSCAN', 'N/A', 'hdbscan not installed'))\n",
   974 +    "\n",
   975 +    "sil_comparison = pd.DataFrame(results, columns=['Method', 'Silhouette Score', 'Notes'])\n",
   976 +    "show(sil_comparison, 'Silhouette Scores Across Clustering Methods (Appendix D1)')"
   977 +   ]
   978 +  },

  1037 +    "    # Use log scale for readability on skewed distributions\n",

  1039 +    "    plot_data[col] = np.log1p(plot_data[col])\n",
  1040 +    "    sns.boxplot(\n",
  1041 +    "        x='Cluster_Label', y=col, data=plot_data,\n",
  1042 +    "        order=label_order, palette='viridis', ax=ax\n",
  1043 +    "    )\n",
  1044 +    "    ax.set_title(title)\n",
  1045 +    "    ax.set_xlabel('')\n",
  1046 +    "    ax.set_ylabel(f'log(1 + {col})')\n",
  1047 +    "    ax.tick_params(axis='x', rotation=15)\n",
  1048 +    "\n",
  1049 +    "fig.suptitle('Distribution of Key Metrics by Cluster (Appendix D7)', fontsize=14, y=1.01)\n",
  1050 +    "fig.tight_layout()\n",
  1051 +    "fig.savefig('fig/cluster_boxplots.pdf', bbox_inches='tight')\n",
  1052 +    "plt.show()"
